<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">бутафо́рия</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">butafórija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***бутерброд.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бутерброд.html>бутербро́д</a> (5337)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Butterbrot</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">open sandwich, slice of bread with butter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">butter bread</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бутерброд.html>бутербро́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">butɛrbród, buterbród</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бутерброд.html>бутербро́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бутерброд.html>бутербро́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бутерброд.html>бутербро́дов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sandwich <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">especially an open sandwich</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1983</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Samuil_Marshak" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Samuil Marshak">Samuil Marshak</a>,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:баллада.html>Балла́да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:королевский.html>короле́вском</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бутерброд.html>бутербро́де</a></cite>  | <cite>Ballad of the King's Bread</cite> | , translation of <cite>The King’s Breakfast</cite> by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A._A._Milne" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:A. A. Milne">A. A. Milne</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">— <a href = vnd.unilang:никто.html>никто́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>ска́жет</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:будто.html>бу́дто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> / <a href = vnd.unilang:тиран.html>тира́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сумасброд.html>сумасбро́д</a>, / <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>За</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чай.html>ча́ю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>люблю́</a> / <a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хоро́ший</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бутерброд.html>бутербро́д</a></b>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">— Niktó ne skážet, búdto ja / Tirán i sumasbród, / Za tó, što k čáju ja ljubljú / Xoróšij <b>butɛrbród/buterbród</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">“No one would say that I / Am a tyrant and madman, / For the fact that with my tea I like / A good <b>bread-and-butter sandwich</b>.”</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">butelka</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">bouteille</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bottle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бутыль.html>буты́ль</a> (10177)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">bouteille</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бутыль.html>буты́ль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">butýlʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бутыль.html>буты́ли</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бутыль.html>буты́ли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бутыль.html>буты́лей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>a large bottle; carboy, demijohn, flask</li></ol>

***бухать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бухать.html>буха́ть</a> (16426)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*buxati</i>, originally onomatopoeic.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бухать.html>бу́хать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">búxatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бухнуть.html>бу́хнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to thump, to bang</li>
<li><i>cannons</i> to thunder, to thud</li>
<li>to let fall with a thud</li>
<li>to blurt out</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>According to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vladimir_Dal" class="extiw" title="w:Vladimir Dal">Vladimir Dal</a> it is related to the homograph <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бухать.html>бу́хать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">búxatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бухать.html>буха́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">buxátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бухнуть.html>бухну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to drink, to booze, to tipple</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бухать.html>бу́хать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">búxatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бухнущий.html>бу́хнущий</a> (14833)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бухнущий.html>бу́хнущий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">búxnuščij</span>)
</p>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Bucht</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бухта.html>бу́хта</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">búxta</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бухта.html>бу́хты</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бухта.html>бу́хты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бухта.html>бу́хт</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bay, inlet</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">bocht</i>.

***бушевать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бушевать.html>бушева́ть</a> (8055)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Derived from either <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:буйный.html>бу́йный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bújnyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wild, unruly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бухнуть.html>бу́хнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">búxnutʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to beat heavily</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">buszować</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бушевать.html>бушева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">buševátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to rage, to storm</li></ol>

***бы.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a> (37)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>The word was the third-person singular aorist of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bytʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, an otherwise obsolete Russian tense (see <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">бꙑти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">byti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Particle">Particle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">by</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">A verbal particle used to render conditional and subjunctive patterns</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́л</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja govoríl.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I spoke.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́л</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>by</b> govoríl.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I would (should) have spoken.; I would speak.; I might speak.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The particle <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a></b> is often shortened to <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">б</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">b</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li>
<li>The particle <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a></b> may come before or after the verb it is targeting.</li>
<li>The particle <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a></b> is often omitted in colloquial settings. For example:</li></ul>
<dl><dd><ul><li><a href = vnd.unilang:словно.html>сло́вно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a> → <a href = vnd.unilang:словно.html>сло́вно</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a>)</li></ul></dd></dl>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>ка́к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kák by ne</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бывалый.html>быва́лый</a> (9670)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps derived from the past tense of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бывать.html>быва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">byvátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to take place, to happen, to be (regularly)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бывалый.html>быва́лый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">byvályj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> worldly-wise, experienced
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бывалый.html>быва́лый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:солдат.html>солда́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>byvályj</b> soldát</i> ― <span class="e-translation">veteran</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> habitual, familiar
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бывалый.html>быва́лое</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éto délo <b>byváloje</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">this is nothing new</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Short forms <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">*<a href = vnd.unilang:бывать.html>быва́л</a>, *<a href = vnd.unilang:бывать.html>быва́ла</a>, *<a href = vnd.unilang:бывать.html>быва́ло</a>, *<a href = vnd.unilang:бывалый.html>быва́лы</a></span> theoretically exist, but are usually avoided due to their similarity to past-tense forms (compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бывать.html>быва́л</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">byvál</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">it took place, it happened, he was (regularly)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, feminine <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бывать.html>быва́ла</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">byvála</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:небывалый.html>небыва́лый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nebyvályj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***бывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бывать.html>быва́ть</a> (265)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бывать.html>быва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">byvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:побывать.html>побыва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to occur, to happen <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">rarely, sometimes, regularly, or often</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to be at, to visit, to stay with
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:побывать.html>побыва́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pobyvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быдло.html>бы́дло</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">býdlo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быдло.html>бы́дла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быдло.html>бы́дла</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быдло.html>бы́дл</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бык.html>бык</a> (3779)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bykъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бык.html>бык</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">byk</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бык.html>быка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бык.html>быки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бык.html>быко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bull, ox</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a big, strong, or stubborn man</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> gangster, mobster, soldier <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">rank-and-file member of a criminal gang</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> abutment, pier</li></ol>

***быль.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:быль.html>быль</a> (24139)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bylь</i>. Synchronically analysable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:щупальце.html>-ль</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:былой.html>было́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bylój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быль.html>быль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bylʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ли</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быль.html>бы́лей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>true story, fact</li>
<li>bylina, epic story</li></ol>
